 unhone kendra sarkaar se jald se jald rashtriya bhoomi sudhaar niti laane kii maang karte hue kaha he ki rajya sarkaar bhi ise puri tarah se lagu karegi

 chouhan ne samvaadadaataaon se baatcheet main kaha ki unki rajya sarkaar sangeen maamalon ko chhodkar adivaasiyon par se sabhi mukademe waapas legi
 The comments ullekhneey he ki jan satyagraiyon kii maangon par dilli main somvaar or phir mangalvaar ko andolankariyon ke pratinidhiyon or kendriya gramin vikaas mantri jairam ramesh ke bich vaarta ho chuki he or kuch muddon par sahmati ban bhi chuki he
 Ramesh can reach Agra among the Satyagrahis on October 11 and declare his demands met
 vah bhi satyagraiyon ke saath paidal chalenge

 yahaan par kai log hajaaron rupee ke pataakhe kharidte hue dikhaai diye
 When people were asked about it, they said that without firecrackers, they cannot celebrate Diwali
 isliye pataakhe bhi kharid lete hai
 Anyway, the Supreme Court has prohibited the selling of firecrackers, not the bursting
 ilaake main kaidukandaar pataakhe bechate najar aae

 media kii khabaron par to ham dukaan nahin band kar sakate
 We will close the shop as soon as the order comes to us

 ham ek baar phir court jaaenge
